Spring and Autumn Summer Coolness

Tidbits 140

— (Yinhu)

People who are always around ninety (degrees) have all gone to escape the summer heat. Those without money, though wiping away buckets of sweat, must still work, and when they find a space, they also need to cool off. Though the situations are different, everyone can enjoy the pleasure.

Those with money go to the high mountains, where the valley breeze comes, cooling the heart and spleen; it is indeed especially comfortable. People who are... between the flowing waters of the countryside, with willow banks and gentle breezes, a bright moon and quiet people, is also enough for one to enjoy the summer.

Racing in cars on the brightly lit avenues might not be as good as drifting in a small boat, leisurely in the middle of the river, with the river breeze and mountain moon, allowing one to dissipate one's worries.

In magnificent buildings, turning on electric fans and eating ice cream, and sitting under a melon trellis, waving a palm-leaf fan, and eating chilled watermelon are each wonderfully enjoyable.

Watermelon 141

— Xiaochu

Watermelon with seeds like snowflakes and silk is the best quality. The ones with thin skin and deep green color are the genuine article. They taste sweet, have plenty of water, and are cool and refreshing in the mouth, enough to dispel summer heat and cleanse the chest. Nothing compares to it. When you raise a knife to cut it open, the sound is crisp, and juice flows everywhere, the fragrance filling the nose. The seeds are arranged in neat rows of black and white, and when chewed, there is no residue to spit out. This is the best of watermelons.

According to experienced watermelon growers, the most important thing is to choose the seeds. If the seeds are bad, even if the planting is done well, there will be no good fruit. Moreover, the influence can spread to other watermelons. Even if you have good seeds, they will gradually become inferior. Because watermelons are formed by cross-pollination, you must be careful when planting. Secondly, it is important to press down the vines. About twenty pools per acre is the rate. Each plant should have its vines pressed down in more than ten places. This way, the roots will be buried deep in the soil and get a thick foundation. One plant can produce seven or eight watermelons. Too many and the watermelons won't be big. There is also a difference in timing. The first ones to form are the "head vine" watermelons, followed by the "...vine" watermelons, and the last are the "final vine" watermelons. The quality is then lower. Thirdly, fertilization is essential. In botanical terms, watermelons belong to the gourd family, which likes to be nourished. Some planters save money by using pig manure, which makes the watermelons taste sour. If human waste is used, this problem doesn't occur. The most particular growers use dog feces or pigeon manure, which makes the northern melon (referring to a high quality watermelon) incomparable. Fourthly, it depends on the weather. If there is a severe drought like last year, watering morning and evening takes a lot of effort, but the watermelons will be numerous, and the harvest will be good. If the rain doesn't come when it should, not only will the fruits easily fall off after flowering, but also it will be hard to get a sweet watermelon. Therefore, the success of the watermelon harvest varies from year to year. This is the general picture.

In terms of location, Shanghai watermelons are most famous from Sanlintang. In the past, Zhaishan, Qiaohaiyuan Market, and Hexing were also quite famous. However, Sanlintang has green-skinned and black-skinned varieties. The green-skinned ones are often snowy, and the black-skinned ones are often red and yellow. There is a type of watermelon that is smaller in shape, with a slightly lighter skin color and fine stripes. It is called a foreign watermelon. It is sweet, with red seeds and extremely thin skin. It is also a good variety. As for making watermelon lanterns, the pulp is removed, and floral patterns are carved on the outside, with a candle lit inside, hanging in the corridor, which is very attractive. It is also an indispensable pleasure for cooling off in the summer nights, so I mention it to give watermelon enthusiasts a try.

Cold Drinks 142

— Zhou Xian

In hot weather, everyone loves to have some cold drinks.

Speaking of cold drinks, there is naturally no city with more than ours. Just ice cream alone has prices ranging from high-end to suit the palates of the first-class people, while at the same time, there are also ones that are affordable for people in the lowest social classes. Naturally, between the most expensive and the cheapest, there are still three levels and nine grades. No matter what class of people you are, there is ice cream that suits your status to eat. Although the high-end ice cream is said to have only one or two thousand bacteria in each cup, and the low-end ice cream is said to have thirty or fifty thousand bacteria in each cup, it's not uncommon, but the ice cream business, whether high-end or low-end, is equally prosperous.

The same goes for shaved ice. In cafes, waitresses carry it on porcelain plates, selling shaved ice. On the streets, cups that cost twenty copper coins also sell shaved ice. Even more grassroots, those carrying a tattered straw bag, shouting in the alleys, "Cold drink! Selling ice!" Although what they sell, who knows if it's machine-made ice or natural ice, but the work they do of "relieving thirst and cooling off" is the same.

Soda is naturally also a blessing in the summer, but following soda, there's fresh orange juice. Following fresh orange juice, there's mineral water. This has the effect of relieving inflammation and cooling off, that has the effect of relieving heat and driving away煩惱，and even more people are praising what kind of water can invigorate the spleen and stomach, and what kind of water can cure diseases and prolong life. We really don't know how many wooden fish we broke in our previous lives, but in this life, we get to enjoy these good flavors.

In addition, there are also "Cool Mint Mung Bean Soup," "Authentic Beijing Plum Juice." And, um, I can't remember all of them for a moment. In short, there are so many, all of which are cold drinks that are both cooling, hygienic, and delicious. You can pick and choose whatever you want to drink and eat.

However, peddlers and coolies always put their mouths to the tap and drink greedily as if drinking sweet dew and jade nectar. If it weren't for these peddlers and coolies having a strange fondness for tap water, then I think that even though there are so many cold drinks in this city, there would at least still be some people feeling left out!

Be Vigilant in Preventing Epidemics 143

— Juan Yin

Hot Window Cold Words 145

— Huoxueming

Sleeping on a cool, smooth bamboo mat, yet pearls of sweat still steam out, how can one not, upon waking in the morning, first cast a glance at the sky? Behold the azure blue, clear clouds, both fixed and far away; even if there is a clump of gray cloud, it will soon dissipate like smoke. Thinking that a sudden downpour will not immediately be unleashed, the greasy sweat seeps out from within the skin. Appreciating closely, even if one's own flesh is not tender: in fact, this magical transformation, leaping out miraculously point by point, can indeed add some miscellaneous interest. If a clump of gray cloud on the horizon becomes denser and darker, and the area also becomes larger, for fear of the heat; my heart flies into the sweet-smelling lake breeze. I only hope that the willows outside dance wildly, the sun is blown out, the gray clouds fly to the treetops, transforming into clear tears, flowing from the willow eyes, green rain, green wind, green world; is there enough peace? Enough that hasn't been cleared? I can no longer spare any emotion to further think of the Yellow River in flood, the Yangtze River overflowing, and what will happen after the cotton seedlings rot. Because everyone in the world is pathetically selfish. Yet can you—?

You must reflect carefully! In the current scorching heat of the world, like a melting furnace, everyone is a piece of iron, burning red. Almost no one's body is not scorching in the harsh heat flow, you scorch me, I scorch you; dancing on thorns, singing under the iron hammer, being baked until unbearable, being beaten until unbearable; yet one should endure, one should smile, one should carve out one's own soul. Even if you can no longer bear this heat, this beating, you cannot escape this melting furnace.

Furthermore, there is indeed a corner of the world, buried in the vast cold water: fishing boats are rowing on the streets, the city walls are submerged at the bottom of the boats; the mountain peaks are full of people, holding their bellies, waiting for the gods; children are pulling on their mothers' sleeves, crying, stretching out withered fingers, yet mothers have no way, and cruelly push their children down the mountain, like rotten, hot apples, "thump" a hit, drifting into the waves; then they themselves fall down and die. Even the birds and beasts that perch on the islands, disturbed by the people, also fly to hot places to live. - Thinking, thinking of this sad picture of "the end of the water," even if you are full of fire, isn't your heart already frozen! May everyone close their eyes, like silently reciting "Namo Amitabha"; silently reciting what history will come after the great floods of the twentieth year of the Republic!

Safe Sea Bathing 146

— Peiyu

The weather is too hot, and sea bathing is in season again. The sea bathing beaches have already opened, waiting for us to dissipate the sweltering heat. However, there are several ways to prevent danger that people who like sea bathing must pay attention to; especially people who are not very healthy and are older, and those who have done very strenuous work and have not yet recovered from their fatigue should be cautious. Such people should not rush to take a sea bath before they have had sufficient time to rest, or before they have acclimatized themselves to the new environment. You should also not go into the sea less than three hours after a meal; because going bathing with a stomach full of food is like inviting disaster to come.

The ears must be protected. It is best to wear a well-fitting soft cap or plug them with cotton; otherwise, the force of the waves will damage the eardrums inside the ears. It is better to bathe at high tide than at low tide, because low tide is close to the beach, and the beach can transmit the heat obtained from the sun's rays to the sea water. If you feel cold on your body, it is a clear sign that you have stayed in the sea water for too long. In this case, the time spent in the water should be reduced; if you feel cold, then sea bathing should be avoided. In short, sea bathing should not cause any discomfort. If you cannot feel absolutely comfortable, it is a smart idea not to take a sea bath; otherwise, you may not be able to withstand the stimulus you encounter.

Before or after a sea bath, it is even more beneficial to wear a swimsuit that exposes the chest and back, and take a sunbath or outdoor exercise. If the sunlight is strong, just wear a cool hat on your head and a pair of sunglasses on your nose. The first day you lie in the sun's rays should be shorter, about five to ten minutes. Showering after bathing can not only remove all the dirt from the body, but also promote and improve blood circulation.

Sea water contains many valuable salts, which increase and accelerate blood circulation when stimulated by cold water, making it easier for our bodies to excrete dirt from the skin. Moreover, the waves hitting our bodies can have the same effect as a strong massage. Therefore, a healthy sea bather should be struck by the waves as much as possible, especially on the back and limbs.

Summer Night 147

— Xingsheng

In this hot summer, everyone feels a sense of depression. But when night comes, the scorching sun hides its tracks, and a cool breeze slowly arrives, bringing a refreshing change of air. After we have been working hard and sweating all day, our bodies are exhausted, and our spirits feel dry and dull, we need this refreshing air to regulate us. Therefore, in the summer, everyone welcomes the arrival of night.

Summer nights are ultimately lovely. On the edges of every road or in an alley, you can always see groups of people enjoying the cool. Old and young, men and women, bustling and chatting happily. Some are singing loudly, some are playing the erhu, singing滩簧, some are singing lewd songs such as "Sister, I love you" and "Little boy comes into the room." Perhaps, this is the only way they think to cool off in this lovely summer night! However, a thoughtful person who hears it will feel the "a courtesan does not know the hatred of a fallen nation, still singing courtyard flowers across the river!"

There are also some young men and women who are usually not very easy to approach. In the summer night, they can take advantage of the opportunity to enjoy the cool to talk about love with the people they are interested in; plus, the thin clothes cling tightly to the body, revealing an alluring sensuality everywhere. People are the most sensual and spiritual animals, so how can they not be captivated? Therefore, in this summer night, you can find men and women chasing, hugging, kissing, joking, and other such romantic cases anytime, anywhere.

Ah! Summer night, ultimately lovely; at the same time, it is also a mysterious night!

Little Knowledge

Icebox Notes 149

— Chuyu

In middle-class families in big cities, almost everyone has an icebox to prevent food spoilage and for the convenience of cold drinks and food. However, there are several points to pay attention to when using an icebox: (1) Do not let the cold air inside the box leak out too much, that is, do not open and close the box door frequently, so that the hot air from the outside flows in, and the temperature drops sharply. The entry and exit of stored items must be very rapid. (2) When storing warm things in the box, cover the top of the container with white cloth or thin paper, so as not to let the dew caused by the hot air fall on the food and damage the flavor of the food. When storing fresh chicken, fish, and meat, put ice on top to keep the fresh flavor. (3) The amount of ice used varies depending on the type and quantity of food, and the number of times the box door is opened and closed. For the first two or three days, put more ice, and then put a certain amount every morning. Then, you can keep the internal temperature evenly and will not change greatly. (4) The inside of the box should be kept dry and clean, and not be damp. Wash it with boiling water three or four times a month. If there is a foul smell or fatty smell, wash it with soap and boiling water. (5) If there is water melted from ice in the box, wipe it off immediately, because ice water reduces the coldness and is extremely unsanitary. The drainage hole should be washed clean frequently to prevent dirt from accumulating. Sawdust and the like that are夹在冰上, wash it clean before putting it in the box. The drainage hole is often blocked by dirt, emitting a foul smell, and pests hide there, so be careful. (6) If the亜鉛皮inside the box is沾了油膩，it will rust. Wash it with alkaline water first, then wipe it with 酒精. (7) An ordinary box can maintain 40 degrees Fahrenheit, which is most suitable for storing food. (8) The icebox should be placed away from direct sunlight and near stoves to avoid热传道 and loss of ice consumption. (9) Do not put hot things in the box, because when put in the box, the temperature is different from the temperature in the box, and dew will fall on the food. (10) Milk, fish, and meat should be placed on the bottom layer, and beer and fruit can be placed on the top layer, because the temperature of the bottom layer is the lowest, and the cold air of the ice descends from above due to the specific gravity. As for the effect of ice, it is originally to inhibit the growth of bacteria. At 40 degrees Fahrenheit, it cannot kill bacteria. The amount of water and the structure of the box are very important. For example, if you use 20 pounds of ice, you can keep the icebox at 52 degrees Fahrenheit. If the ice melts to 15 pounds, the temperature will rise to 60 degrees. If it melts to 10 pounds, the temperature will rise to 70 degrees, so the ice in the box should be replenished frequently, so that the original temperature can be maintained. The relationship between bacterial growth and temperature is as follows: in one day and night, at 40 degrees Fahrenheit, bacteria can multiply 9 grains, 45 degrees 13 grains, 50 degrees 39 grains, 55 degrees 90 grains, 60 degrees 110 grains. From this, we can know that as the temperature rises, the bacteria multiply faster.

Ministry of Education Instructs Hebei: Improve Two Provincial Colleges 163

The Ministry of Education issued instructions to the Hebei Provincial Agricultural College on the 26th, stating: "The college has previously been instructed to improve based on the key points raised by this department. Upon reviewing the report of the inspectors this time, the professors' various research experiments at the college have been found to be diligent. They have also paid attention to the various difficulties pointed out by the Ministry. However, the following highlights still need to be improved: 1. The college's curriculum still lacks a general physics course, which should be established immediately. A physics laboratory, soil laboratory, and greenhouse are necessary facilities for agricultural science and should be added in order. The Physics Laboratory at the Hebei Medical College is also lacking, so the two colleges can temporarily negotiate to jointly organize and use it. 2. The college's research work has been paying attention to the needs of the province. In the future, they should establish contact with the agricultural experimental fields of the Provincial Department of Construction to seek promotion. This is hereby ordered for compliance and reporting."

On the same day, the Ministry of Education also instructed the Hebei Provincial Medical College, stating: "The college has previously been instructed to improve based on the key points raised by this department. Upon reviewing the report of the inspectors this time, the college is still planning to improve the points raised by this department. The following key points are now listed for reporting and handling: 1. The college should add a public health department within the possible range of funding to meet local needs, and appropriately increase the equipment of the midwifery class and expand it into a nursing midwifery department. 2. If the college's internship facilities cannot be fully equipped at once, it may temporarily negotiate cooperation methods with the local Si Luo Hospital and the Health Education Department of the Dingxian Chinese Semi-Civil Education Promotion Association to provide internships. 3. The college's training management officials should strictly implement the established implementation methods and encourage teachers to provide guidance in order to cultivate the ability to serve society in the future. This order is hereby given," etc.

The Chinese Mathematical Society continued to hold its meeting yesterday at the Jiaoda Library, with over forty members in attendance. Municipal Education Bureau Summer School: Lecture Period Ends Today; Yesterday, Wang Yukai Gave Lecture on Public Training 168

The Municipal Education Bureau Summer School and Summer Training Session invited Mr. Wang Yukai, who recently returned from the United States, to give a lecture on civic training yesterday. Mr. Wang first introduced civic training in various countries, including England, Germany, France, the United States, and Japan. He then explained that current civic training in China should focus on (1) literacy education, (2) fully developing scientific knowledge, (3) skills for making a living, (4) sinicized habits, and (5) having a clear national consciousness. His thorough explanation was considered a good plan for citizenship. The lecture lasted two hours, and over eight hundred students listened attentively and took notes in the hot weather, showing great interest. All the audience applauded to express their respect. Mr. Wang lectured at the International Academy of California for a year, promoting Chinese culture with tireless efforts. He also represented China at the International Problems Research Conference, working hard for the country. His contributions are great. Furthermore, the summer school's lecture period ends today, and all students will leave the school.

Shanghai Municipal Council: Preparing to Add Chinese Children's Schools 169

Regarding the increase in Chinese education facilities in the Public Concession, the Director of Finance presented a report at the last meeting of the Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating that he had repeatedly and carefully considered the issue of increasing Chinese children's schools. According to his opinion, if no unexpected events occur beforehand, he could recommend adding a Chinese children's primary school at 170 Wenjianshi Road in the budget for the following year. The school could open in the spring of the year, with annual expenses set at 35,000 to 40,000 yuan. This expense could be partially raised from other savings items, but this amount is actually the maximum increase in education expenses for 1936. The Education Department was very satisfied after hearing the report from the Director of Finance and immediately recorded it. They also plan to consult with the Works Department on matters related to renovating the building so that the plan can be quickly prepared for opening after it is approved by the Board of Directors.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Scout Troop is the only and most effective troop in Shanghai for training young businessmen. Gold Market Price Exceeds Standard Price 176

Rumors of the collapse of silver cause a rally after an initial decline, nearing the $70 mark, ultimately rising $7.40

The gold market initially weakened yesterday but then strengthened. Declines were difficult, while increases were still easy. Overseas silver markets were flat. Dealers were constrained by the standard gold price, partly because it was assumed that if China implemented inflation, gold prices could not rise as sharply as other commodities. Later, rumors of a severe drop in Indian silver reappeared, but this pushed the price near the $70 mark, higher than the closing price. In the early morning, overseas silver markets and forward silver prices were stable. Exchange rates were slightly higher. London gold rose one penny. Sentiment was normal. Off-market pre-open trading opened lower at $58.90. Sellers were still eager, retreating to $7. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with the British pound unchanged and the US dollar rising. The Customs Gold Unit rose three li, pushing the standard gold price to $867.80. Sentiment slightly improved, rising to $8.90. The morning opening was still low, but there was a slight rise after the opening. Banks offered a lot of sales, repeatedly dumping. Exchange rates turned firm, finally moving upwards. HSBC's posted rates were announced, with both British and American currencies unchanged. After falling, there was a significant rebound. The price fluctuations were intricate, but the situation was peaceful. National banks purchased forward shillings. Chinese merchants were eager to buy, and the exchange rate suddenly tightened. Buyers moved in concert, breaking through the $60 mark. There were rumors of certain banks entering the market, boosting confidence and causing the price to rise. However, because banks took the opportunity to sell at high prices, the process was tight and then loosened, briefly falling back within the $60 mark. Nevertheless, sentiment had improved, and buying interest remained strong. Predictions of Indian silver falling by five annas finally caused another rise. The exchange market was normal, and major players supplied at high prices. The market stabilized at noon. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was stable. Although buying interest was strong, banks took advantage of the high prices to sell. The Dalian shipping companies continued to sell, and although prices rose, the progress was extremely slow. When the initial announcement came that Indian silver had fallen by eleven annas, sentiment became even firmer. Banks sold and then bought back. The exchange market suddenly tightened, and buying interest surged. Rumors of inside trading reappeared, causing repeated increases, pushing the price above the standard gold price, and briefly nearing the $70 mark. Banks took advantage of the high prices to sell, and major players also liquidated their holdings. As a result, although Indian silver continued to fall for the second time, there was still a slight setback. After the defeat, the market remained active.

Publishing World

Cultural Movement and Revolutionary Movement 190

— Yu Shi

Just as general metaphysical idealists fail to understand the relationship between revolutionary movements and cultural movements, so too do general mechanical materialists fail to understand the relationship between cultural movements and revolutionary movements.

In the eyes of general mechanical materialists, cultural movements and revolutionary movements are two completely irreconcilable and opposing movements. The opposition between these two movements is like the opposition between centrifugal force and centripetal force, always repelling each other at one end.

Are cultural movements and revolutionary movements truly opposed? I am very skeptical of this confused assertion.

The first thing I want to point out to the public is that revolutionary movements are by no means a simple action that can encompass everything. Kropotkin, in his great work "The Great French Revolution," begins by saying: Two great currents prepared and brought about the French Revolution. One is the current of thought; the other is the current of action. The combination of these two currents resulted in revolution. In fact, not only the French Revolution, but all modern revolutions are the result of the convergence of ideological currents and action currents. From this point of view, isn't opposing ideological and cultural movements opposing revolutionary movements as well?

Secondly, all revolutions do not develop in a straight line. Especially after a revolution suffers setbacks, if the revolution wants to revive, it must go through a new stage of ideological and cultural movement.

Without discussing distant events, how effectively our "May Fourth" New Culture Movement revived our first revolutionary movement should still be in everyone's memory. If forgetful people have even forgotten this historical fact, then please have them read recent history.

In my view, the ideological and cultural movement that has just begun to unfold is not opposing the Chinese revolution; on the contrary, it is paving the way for the future Chinese revolution. After the people have gone through the practical lessons of the past six or seven years, the people not only demand a change in the current state of the nation, but also demand a change in themselves—to make their own knowledge development more suitable for future social movements. This is the true meaning of the current ideological and cultural movement. From this, it can be seen that ideological and cultural movements not only do not hinder revolution, but are the greatest preparers and organizers of future revolutions. Without it, the revolution might just die.

Which ideological and cultural movement in history has not been the precursor to national awakening?

We cannot simply view the current cultural movement from a sectarian point of view as the result of some conspiracy or strategy. We should view it from the perspective of the entire historical development as the inevitable requirement of the present historical moment. This is the manifestation of the people consciously changing the desperate and erroneous movements of the past on a larger scale. This is the manifestation of the people reopening the revolutionary ocean after the ship of revolution has sailed into a dead harbor. This is the manifestation of the people attempting to revive and grow the revolution on a national and societal scale after revolutionary alchemists who followed unorthodox paths have ruined the revolution.

Just as the "May Fourth Ideological and Cultural Movement" revived the dead first revolution, the current ideological and cultural movement has the great historical mission of reviving the future Chinese revolution.

Past mistakes, and the serious consequences resulting from these mistakes, have not only brought the people to a loss, but have even led the people to a state of numbness and apathy. The heart of the nation has fallen into a state of paralysis. How can you ask its limbs to dance for you? Can you use the manipulative techniques of a puppeteer to make them dance for you without using the enlightening means of an ideological and cultural movement? As we know, puppeteers can use their unique techniques to make puppets make gestures to the audience, but this is by no means a pure and great historical drama, but merely a performance by江湖 entertainers!

Indiscriminately opposing cultural movements, and even opposing reading and literacy movements, is a completely soulless act. It is the most sad, morbid, tyrannical, and despicable manifestation of arrogance in this era. I hope that this kind of performance will never happen again.

In my view, developing the current ideological and cultural movement and raising the national level of knowledge is not only necessary for the revival of the Chinese revolution, but also very necessary for those backward, functionally atrophied revolutionary alchemists.

From Writing a Book to Publishing a Book (II) 191

— Qi Zhong

Typesetting

Entering the typesetting room, one sees rows and rows of type cases, arranged like elementary school students lining up, containing type sizes such as No. 1, No. 2, No. 3, No. 4, No. 5, and No. 6, just like the grades from first to sixth in elementary school. The most widely used are No. 5 and No. 6 types. The arrangement of these rows of type cases is based on the radicals in the dictionary, with slight modifications. When we outsiders go up and want to find a required character, we spend half a day without success. The skilled workers, however, run around to retrieve the characters and can pick up about eight hundred characters per hour, which will undoubtedly surprise you.

In addition to the type cases, there are also trays and trays of "punctuation marks," "symbols," "blank leads," "lead strips," and "lead wires," arranged on the table. Skilled workers do not even need to look at them with their eyes, but simply pick them up with their hands. These are prepared for page makeup.

The first step in typesetting is "character retrieval" (called "picking rough castings" in their workshop). A specialized character retrieval worker, according to the type size specified on the original manuscript, takes the required characters from the type case and places them one by one in the type box, according to the predetermined number of characters per line. If a character is not in the type case or cannot be found temporarily, a blank lead or ink chip is placed there, or another character is placed upside down or sideways, for correction after proofreading. After the character retrieval worker retrieves the characters, another worker adds punctuation marks and embeds lead strips and lead wires to make it the same size as the predetermined page opening. This is called page makeup. After the page is made up, it is sent to the proofing frame to print a sample, which is sent to the proofreader to proofread according to the original manuscript.

Here, I will say a few more words about machine typesetting: What I said before was Chinese typesetting. As for typesetting Western languages, because Western languages have only a small number of letters, manual typesetting does not require the character retrieval worker to run around like Chinese typesetting. They can sit down and work. As for machine typesetting, it is like typing on a typewriter. As you type the original text, new lead characters are cast one by one and jump out to be arranged for you in the character box. Therefore, this kind of typesetting machine does not require pre-casting lead characters; they are all cast temporarily. Some people have tried to invent a machine for typesetting Chinese characters using this method, but after all, because Chinese characters are not phonetic and there are too many characters, they could not invent it, which shows that Chinese characters do need to be improved.

Proofreading

The first step of proofreading is called "rough proofreading," which is usually handled by the typesetting room. This rough proofreading is only to correct the missing characters on the sample, so that the sample does not become full of black dots. As for the style, etc., that is not their concern. This kind of rough proofreading work,

Reader, you will say that proofreading is just correcting typos, this work is very easy. However, reader, if you think so, that is wrong; because the proofs are not very clear, it is easy to make people dizzy. We often see books that are printed very clearly, but there is often a typo in them that we look over without noticing. How can looking at a proof full of typos not make people dizzy! If a printing bureau does not have a "troubleshooting" rough proofreading master, then the proofreaders will certainly be even more miserable!

Ordinary proofreading is mostly done three times. The first time is called the first proofreading. The proofreader unfolds the proof and looks at the original manuscript character by character. The wrong characters are corrected, the extra characters are deleted, and the omissions are added. At the same time, attention must also be paid to the format and page opening. This first proofreading is the most painful, because there are many typos, which easily make people dizzy. After the proofreading is done, the proof is sent back to the printing bureau, and the printing bureau corrects them one by one, and then prints another sample to send back for proofreading. This is called the second proofreading. The second proofreading is much easier, although there are still inevitably "problems" and typos, but it is not as chaotic as the first proofreading, so proofreading is also easier. However, if the proofreader does not know the proofreading skills, and the correction symbols used cannot be understood by the workers, then you proofread yours, and they correct theirs, resulting in the same mess, still like the first proofreading before it was proofread. It still makes people dizzy. The second proofreading is sent back to the printing bureau, corrected and sent back for proofreading, which is called the third proofreading. If the proofreading is good, there are not many typos in the third proofreading, and it can be signed. However, if a typo was missed during the second proofreading, it can still be corrected. Therefore, the responsibility of the personnel in the third proofreading is very great. However, if a typo is missed in the third proofreading, and you have already signed it and made the paper plates, then there is no way to correct it, and you can only wait until the paper plates are made before digging and correcting them on the paper plates. However, it doesn't matter if you occasionally correct one character on the paper plate, but it is troublesome to correct too many; because correcting paper plates is charged per character. As for the format, it cannot be changed on the paper plate. Therefore, the responsibility of the personnel in the third proofreading is truly great!

Model Making

After the manuscript has been proofread, lead type is used to make paper plates. This is called "model making." Model making is an important step in preparing to print a book, because it is very inconvenient to send the pages typeset with movable type to the machine for printing; moreover, putting so many lead characters on the machine for printing will cause the typesetting room to feel short of resources, and the work will inevitably be affected; furthermore, the lead characters will naturally be damaged by the heavy pressure of the machine during printing, and soon the characters will become blurred and unusable. They become a pile of scrap lead and must be returned to the furnace for melting and recasting new characters, which is a great loss! Also, if you have spent a lot of effort typesetting a page and printed the first edition of a new book, if you don't have paper plates, you must re-typeset and re-proofread, which is not only time-consuming but also expensive. Therefore, making paper plates means that when you reprint, you only need to take out the paper plates and cast them into lead plates. Wouldn't that kill several birds with one stone! Therefore, making paper plates from typeset pages is an indispensable step. (To be continued)

Introducing a Lively Book on Studying Chemistry 192

— Ren You

"Chemical Curiosities," translated by Gu Junzheng, written by Fabre.

Kaiming Publishing Price 90 cents

Most of our educational circles are immersed in dead books. Teachers lecture like gramophones according to the textbooks, and students record the sound like gourds, which is called being a good student. But if you send this good student to a laboratory, he will not know what to do. This is because education has not yet integrated learning and application, especially in the sciences. To solve this difficulty, I would like to solemnly introduce "Chemical Curiosities" to our readers.

Everyone says that chemistry is a boring and difficult subject, but "Chemical Curiosities" gives every reader a wealth of interest. The author writes about mysterious chemistry through the interesting dialogue of the lovable Emile and Jules with their uncle Paul. When we see Uncle Paul's earnest, novel, and loving attitude, this book will make us feel interested in studying. Of course, Fabre would not have been able to write this book if he had not had literary cultivation.

For example, in the third chapter, when he talks about carbon, he does not start from carbon, but starts from a piece of burnt bread to薇, which is so 引人 嚼味!

Also, when he talks about the meaning of chemical combination, he says:

"What does sulfur and iron become after they get married? We cannot call it sulfur, because it is no longer sulfur; we cannot call it iron, because it is no longer iron; we cannot say that it is a mixture of sulfur and iron, because although it was initially a mixture, it is no longer a mixture later. This thing is chemically called iron sulfide, and this term reminds us that these two substances are combined under the constraints of chemical marriage."

He calls chemical combination marriage, which is the most appropriate metaphor. He also比喩 the heat, light, explosion, crackling, and sparks produced during chemical reactions as firecrackers and lanterns to celebrate their marriage, isn't that very interesting?

Mr. Ye Shaojun's preface to this book is the most thorough:

"Although this book, 'Chemical Curiosities,' is also a book, it is not a book to be read, nor is it a book to be 'memorized.' The original author, Fabre, skillfully used his pen to depict the efforts of the '赋' character, so that readers not only have chemical knowledge, but also can do chemical experiments, and at the same time increase their ability to try, which can be used to deal with other things. 'Chemistry'—this term is so boring and tasteless when written on the curriculum, but in this book it is almost the most touching story. 'I can do it like Jules Emile!' the reader will think, and because the experimental equipment is 'readily available' or self-made, the reader will immediately 'do it himself' according to what the book says. And do it more creatively."

"Whoever only 'reads' or 'memorizes' this book is letting this book down."

Young friends who need wisdom, remember this sentence and read this interesting book.

Editor's note: The reason why books on natural science are not very popular in our country is mainly because they are boring and tasteless, not only the theories, but mainly the writing style. Therefore, if we want to popularize natural science knowledge among the general public, we must make this kind of explanatory writing interesting and literary. This requires the reform of the writing style. The editor dares to raise this issue here, hoping to arouse public discussion.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Hygiene Semimonthly

— Edited by Dr. Yuan Yimin

Neurasthenia 193

— Feng Shanliang

Brain Neurasthenia: The brain is the main organ of a person. The exercise of will is all commanded by the pivotal organ. If the brainpower is not strong, everything cannot be fully developed. If hereditary syphilis or alcohol poisoning damages the central nervous system, resulting in dementia (loss of consciousness) and becoming ignorant and insensible, happiness is lost. How can one be human? Brain damage is critical to health. The impact on lifelong happiness is significant. Many modern young people also suffer from neurasthenia. Although the occurrence of this symptom is sometimes due to the destruction of bad habits, it is also caused by congenital deficiency and acquired imbalance. In addition, those who study too hard, work excessively, and are overly sensitive are all at risk of developing this symptom. If ignored arbitrarily, or even excessively harming oneself, it will eventually become an incurable disease.

Sexual Neurasthenia: The irrigation of plants depends on fertilizer, and the cultivation of the human body depends on nutrients. The underdevelopment of reproductive organs is one of these factors. In the end, all blame falls on the parents. When a person is a child, responsibility falls on the parents. Originally, children could have perfect physical health and complete development without any problems, except for paying attention to nutrition and digestion. Unfortunately, from childhood to adulthood, parents do not pay attention and let them develop naturally, resulting in habitual bad habits. How many young people lose their ambition! If attention is paid in advance to investigate whether there are any symptoms or physiological changes, it should be distinguished clearly and corrected early, so that happiness can be maintained. Now, observing young people with weak wills, whose bodies are generally healthy, recklessly engaging in non-actions during the developmental period, their bodies gradually become thin and weak, eventually developing neurasthenia. Symptoms such as poor memory, small reproductive organs, and all phenomena of sexual dysfunction appear immediately. When treating this symptom, in addition to the use of drug treatment, the application of electrotherapy is an indispensable and necessary auxiliary.

Eczema 194

— Dr. Wu Sheng

The areas where eczema is most likely to occur are usually in the joints and genital area, such as the inner thighs, around the scrotum, and the inner side of the upper brain. Sometimes it is scattered on the limbs.

When this symptom occurs, the skin usually feels itchy, burning, and swollen first. Next, papules the size of pinheads develop, gradually turning into blisters. There are also exceptions, either rupturing or forming soft scabs. It is stubborn and difficult to treat.

The causes of this symptom are mostly unclean skin, parasitic bacteria, glandular nausea liquid, and blood circulation disorders. However, it is also due to chemical, thermal, and mechanical stimulation, such as hard laborers being most susceptible to this disease. It is also due to anemia, chlorosis, and diabetes, but it is very rare.

Treatment of this symptom mostly focuses on local treatment. The overall condition must also be considered. For local therapy, it is best to avoid using alcohol-based liquid medicines, as they stimulate the peeling of the epidermis, not only are ineffective, but also harmful. At this time, it is best to use ointments or oils. Diagnosis of Gonorrhea in Women 196

— Dr. Liu Xuan Nu

(1) Diagnosis During the Latent Period: Collect secretions from the patient's urethra, the external os of the uterus, or the uterine cavity using platinum or silver wire. Prepare a smear specimen, stain it, and examine it under a microscope. This will reveal the presence of pathogens and numerous epithelial cells.

(2) Diagnosis During the Prodromal Period: Examine smear specimens collected from various locations using the method described above. Specimens taken from the urethra will reveal the presence of pathogens, epithelial cells, and a small amount of mucus. Specimens taken from the genital organs, specifically the cervical os and the uterine cavity, will show similar findings, but with a greater number of pathogens.

(3) Diagnosis During the Purulent Discharge Period: During this period, a large amount of pus can be seen with the naked eye at the external urethral orifice and within the uterine cavity. Microscopic examination of the epithelial cells from the urethral orifice can confirm the diagnosis of gonorrhea. When gonorrhea is limited to the urethra, the two-glass test is used. Turbidity in the first glass of urine indicates urethritis, while turbidity in the second glass indicates cystitis, pyelitis, or nephritis. For the latter conditions, a three- or four-glass test is used, where all glasses of urine appear turbid.

A Discussion on the Treatment of Gonorrhea 197

— Cui Fuqing

Gonorrhea, commonly known as "white turbidity," accounts for sixty to seventy percent of venereal diseases. It is generally understood to result from unclean sexual intercourse between men and women, or from frequenting brothels. It is caused by a gonococcal bacterium that invades the mucous membrane of the male urethra or the cervix of the female uterus. This bacterium has a strong reproductive capability, quickly causing urinary tract disturbances. Initial symptoms include urethral burning, painful urination, cloudy urine, tissue swelling, and the secretion of a pus-like fluid, or even bleeding, accompanied by a high fever. This is known as acute gonorrhea. If not treated properly, the gonococci will invade the deeper parts of the urethra, leading to chronic gonorrhea. Although the symptoms may appear to subside, with reduced secretion and pain, the root of the disease deepens. The bacteria lie dormant in the deep urethra, and cannot be eradicated by medication in a short time, resulting in lifelong harm, or even sterility and death. Currently, most physicians treating gonorrhea use intravenous injections of yellow dye, or vaginal irrigations with silver protein, Rivarol solutions, such as RERGON, ARGNON, and HEGONON. These treatments can achieve considerable results, but their effectiveness is slow and the issue of complete eradication remains questionable. Injections of yellow dye, typically a 0.5% solution, administered at 10 to 20 cc per injection, can cause nausea and toxic symptoms due to the patient's constitution. Rapid injections can trigger severe acute poisoning, posing considerable danger and requiring careful consideration. In recent years, medicine has advanced rapidly, becoming increasingly refined, thanks to the promotion of science. For example, the shortwave diathermy used at the Chun Zai Hospital at No. 66 Ningbo Road in the French Concession, and MESALTROPIN (Gonorrhea Reduction Tablets) sold by Ren Shou Western Pharmacy at No. 1, Laodexing Lane, Mintiniyin Road, Ba Xian Qiao in the French Concession, are particularly effective for treating acute and chronic gonorrhea in both men and women, as well as all conditions caused by gonorrhea. Furthermore, GONO-SEROL serum, a new product from the German Munel Zhi foreign firm, is an effective medicine for treating gonococcal urethritis. It is easy to use, painless, and can reach the folds of the mucosa and the small fissures within the urethra, allowing the bacteria on the surface and in the deeper layers to be killed simultaneously. In addition to treatment, it also helps prevent "white candles" [a slang term for advanced stages of gonorrhea].

Essays

The Problem of Medical Treatment for the Poor 200

— Meng Ruo

I recently read a Nanjing news report stating: The Municipal Party Department sent a letter to the Municipal Government stating that many doctors in the city were outwardly complying with the standard fee schedule set by the Municipal Government but secretly increasing their charges. It requested strict enforcement and ordered the Health Bureau to conduct regular investigations. Those who do not adhere to the fee schedule and arbitrarily charge more than the prescribed amount should be strictly punished. This is truly a meritorious act.

In addition to the necessary expenses for food, clothing, and shelter, medical expenses are also an indispensable part of a person's living expenses. It is difficult to bear the discomfort of hunger, but the suffering of physical imbalance without medication is even more unbearable. As the saying goes, "Heaven has unpredictable winds and clouds, and people have unexpected misfortunes." Those with strong bodies can still manage, but those with weak bodies are constantly susceptible to disease. The importance of medical expenses is evident.

However, seeing a doctor and taking medicine is not easy. The "not easy" here naturally refers to the majority of poor people. Wealthy people take tonics even when they are not sick, which is a different matter. Perhaps the situation is better in other places, but the high cost of medical care in Shanghai is simply daunting. Needless to say, those with doctorates or famous doctors are not catering to the poor. Even ordinary doctors charge three or two yuan for a consultation, and at least one yuan. Adding the cost of medicine, trying to invite one to come home and see you, the house-call fee is three to five times higher than the consultation fee, plus travel expenses. Sometimes the doctor considers it necessary and gives you one or two injections, the cost of which can be unbearable.

But illness is unavoidable for everyone, which is truly life-threatening. Many poor people cannot afford to see a doctor when they are sick, so they have to struggle with their illness using their own bodies. Surviving is a matter of luck, and not resisting is a matter of fate.

However, there are some charitable organizations in Shanghai that provide free clinics for the poor, not only providing free consultations but also dispensing medicine. They are indeed benefiting the poor, but it is said that many of these clinics are poorly equipped and the consultations are perfunctory. As a result, some people are reluctant to seek help even when they are sick. This really needs to be improved. It should be understood that charitable work should also be done to a considerable degree. We cannot be perfunctory just because we are providing free consultations. We hope that the municipal authorities can build more hospitals for the poor in Shanghai, providing completely free consultations and medications. This would be a very good social undertaking.

The Philosopher 201

— Kemin

—— Sketches of Characters

On the bustling streets in the noisy areas, in the dark corners of the metropolis, in the street-facing windows of low-grade lodgings, or even on the bare sidewalks, a frighteningly small shop front is set up, with elegant titles like "Lay Buddhist" or "Traveler" displayed. Outside, there is a jumbled display of portraits of Song Hongwu, Li Yuanhong, and the great Chinese leader Sun Yat-sen, along with fate charts covered with red circles and detailed annotations, mysterious arrangements of stems and branches, and jargon from the world of fortune-telling. A sign hangs: "Philosopher – Shanren [Hermit] Fortune-Telling Hall"; and on another sign, one sees the cost of the "Philosopher's" services: "Palm Reading Half Yuan, Fate Reading One Yuan..." In addition, there is the "Philosopher" who advertises "Scientific and Philosophical Fortune Telling."

Like all the leftover literate figures in the officialdom, a long gown is very important to them; with it, they can distinguish themselves from the "common people," putting themselves in a higher position than some laborers, desperately squeezing themselves into the ranks of "scholars," squeezing themselves into the circle of "visiting merchants, high-class ladies."

Page 18

.

Yes, from there, they play the role of "men of letters," taking advantage of the difficulties in this increasingly desolate world, taking advantage of the mentality of the petty bourgeoisie who grow up in fatalism. In titles like "Lay Buddhist," "Hermit," "Philosopher," they breathe and write like parasites on a rotten leaf, living from day to day with less and less certainty.

However, it is said that the "Philosopher" may have studied in private schools, primary schools, or middle schools when he was young. Following the old teacher to study the Four Books, the Book of Changes, and the Zuo Zhuan; a scholar is also a "scholar"! But, growing up, relying on empty "words," he cannot make a living in business, and he lacks practical skills. Drifting, floating; fortunately, the people of this ancient country all believe in relying on Heaven for food and on fate for life, so this path may be passable. So, he must first spend hundreds of days "doing" a hand of writing that seems to be "dragons flying and phoenixes dancing," mastering the "jia yi bing ding" [the ten Heavenly Stems], understanding the jargon of the fortune-telling world, raising capital, and setting up the scene. Then, he sits inside, waiting for the believers of fatalism: the disappointed, the struggling, the doubtful and wandering, those who have lost their reason in the inevitable decline of this era... Then, questioning and "pointing out," at this time, the genius of "alertness" is needed, and the skill of "observing words and discerning colors" is also needed. The "Philosopher" must also be a "psychologist," using such "talent" to persuade and intimidate those weak fatalists, trying to gain greater profits from others' desire for security and avoidance of trouble. They live on, live on.

However, times are really bad, and this business is also difficult to do. They have to cope with the competition from the same industry and think of some novel tricks. Recently, even for a devout believer in fatalism, the strange-shaped portrait of Zhu Hongwu and his "True Son of Heaven" "eight characters" are no longer attractive – these days, everything must be new! So, when others put up the sign of "First-Class Literary Doctor," one must also think of a "Philosopher" and "Scientific Fortune Teller" to muddle through. But, no matter how many tricks there are, it is true that business is difficult these days: even if people want to know when they are destined to get rich, the cost of a few cents is enough to think about. In this world, money is the most real.

For this reason, our "Philosopher" must also plan and start "Dog Racing Winning Method" and "Aviation Lottery Purchasing Method" to grab another group of customers, another group of people.

But, what the "Philosopher" can't understand most is: "He is also a scholar, and he doesn't even have a good meal."

This is a "philosophy" that even the "philosopher" does not understand!

Nocturne 202

— By Chen Jingsheng

A Small Feeling Looking at Clouds 203

— Chen Tianshe

I love clouds. Summer is the season of clouds. I love watching the illusions of clouds. The clouds of summer evenings are extraordinarily mysterious and rapidly changing. Each posture of each cloud will not be maintained for even half a minute. When a plein air painter wants to depict a summer evening wilderness, how sensitive a vision and rapid a brushstroke he must use! Moreover, the colors of the summer evening clouds are very complex. Perhaps sometimes the palette will be stumped by the artificial colors used to adapt to the illusions of nature. Even the transcendent artist will inevitably encounter occasional difficulties!

When I was a child in the countryside, I took a bath on summer evenings, lightly wore a beige coarse summer cloth tunic and shorts, put on small wooden clogs, sat on a low bamboo stool in the field, and my mother peeled green beans on the side. The cool breeze shook down from the top of that old cassia tree, carrying the green scent of the leaves. I leisurely held a palm fan that was not needed and watched the sky, watched the floating clouds in the sky. Relying on my own imagination, I would see those clouds as various people or animals. When I was in a daze, I would shout out: "Mom, isn't that a bullock cart over there!"

When my mother was happy, she would also look up. The glow of the sunset illuminated her smooth forehead. Her eyes were green, and there were clouds flowing inside. At that time, my mother was still in her prime. When I pointed to a cloud, dragged her arm, and leaned on her shoulder, entwining with her, she would pretend to be angry and say: "I think you're going to turn into a fool." But in the end, she would always smile so kindly, which I understood. I still wanted to entwine with her: "Mom, isn't that an old woman carrying a load over there." Pointing to the sky.

But, mother gradually aged in the drifting of the clouds. Now, she will not say to me: "The clouds are released from the valley, and the immortals still take them back into the valley." This kind of myth. She still lives with a sickly body hidden in her distant coastal hometown, but I have been blown by the storms of life into this city. Many of my childhood temperaments have been completely lost along the way, and my circumstances are just like the floating clouds of summer evenings, without even a chance to appreciate them for a while, not at all...

"Unfeeling floating clouds, unfeeling years!"

Every time I think about it, I will sigh like this, especially on these summer evenings. I roll up the curtains of the small building, let my tired body after running around during the day lean on the window lattice, hold a cheap cigarette, and, in the bitter taste, look up at the flowing clouds in the sky. To this day, only the interest in watching the clouds has not diminished. I want to reflect my drifting life from the clouds, but my house is too low. In the city, it is not easy to get a wide sky. People living in the city also do not easily have an open mind. Thus, as soon as the bright sunlight comes, it is obscured by the clouds, and the eyes feel a gloom.

"Is that gray cloud floating from the sea sky of my hometown? Has it also passed over the head of my elderly mother? ...Has my mother ever looked up at it, and known that that cloud is going to drift to her son's eyes thousands of miles away?"…

I often question myself like this in my brain.

The taste of the cigarette feels more bitter. I feel that each stage of life is just like the dispersion and illusion of clouds, and will never return to its original state. No one can predict what kind of shape the peony-shaped floating cloud will turn into. Sighing is also useless. You still have to guard against the sudden arrival of a great wind.

Night Flight 204

— Ji Tuan

That day, from dusk, the sky began to gloomily spread out black clouds. Then came terrifying thunder and lightning. Finally, a necessary and unavoidable downpour fell as if poured from the sky.

The heavy rain kept falling, hitting the iron roof of the small house, as rapid as the drums on a battlefield, stirring up people's hearts like swirling muddy water. Looking at the sky, the rain continued to fall, as if vowing to pour down all the moisture that had been lingering in the sky for so long, not leaving a single drop. It was already late at night, yet the rain showed no sign of stopping. However, to me, it seemed like it didn't matter anymore. For the sake of life, I had to immediately throw myself out of the rain-soaked door in the deep night, and head towards the metropolis hundreds of miles away. All the attachments and reluctance had been completely shattered in the search for a livelihood. I had to brave the darkness of the night, the rain of the night, and throw myself out.

My wife blessed me, packed my luggage, put a raincoat on me, lit the hand lantern to illuminate the dark alley, opened the door for me, and entrusted me with laughter and tears to take care of myself. And I, certainly, had to rush without hesitation into the land of the night.

(There's no need to say any more about love, affection, and other such terms. We are both young—yes. But haven't we learned enough from the hardships of life in the past year or two? People shouldn't have feelings—why should people have them? How happy a person would be without feelings...)

When we were young (but is it old age now?), we all had a pair of eyes and a soul. And when we discovered that this world was not very suitable for those with eyes and souls to live in, we all acted childishly in the face of life, made up our minds, and resolutely broke away from the repulsive face of the world, stubbornly coming to this simple place, intending to use our own labor and enthusiasm as fertilizer to irrigate this even simple life. It doesn't have to be a successful and lush tree; even the finest young sprout would be satisfying.

However, "What a silly idea!" People of this era are very concerned about life and do not pay attention to anything outside of it. (Within the circle of life, they are refined, sensitive, cunning, and capable; but outside the circle of life, they are fools and ignorant people, they are...) So, the days went by, and life became more and more difficult. At this time, the world understood people, and people also understood the world.

But the meaning of life is "to eat," and not just willow-like floating catkins! In these days, two young people have suffered enough for the sake of life. When there is no longer a chance to remember the ugliness of the world, people have already hesitated on the edge of hunger and no longer think about anything.

Then understand: It should be a time to worry again. We are no longer the smallest children, fearing the outside world, even if it is without sin, but it is dangerous—life never lies or jokes with people, it deals with people with a straight face!

In this way, what else is there to miss other than the days to come—whether it is terrible, ugly, or the suffering of difficult parting, life requires you to drift away, and people cannot (or should not) resist, yes!

Learning to be without feeling, I think, may not be difficult? And it is said that being without feeling is often happiness. Then, what does the night, the heavy rain, or the tears of farewell from family members have to do with anything? The night is spread out endlessly outside, the rain still hasn't stopped, the road is dark and muddy, and I, finally braving the rain, braving the night, have run far away.

Revised on July 10, 1925

Night Stay at Songbin 205

— Rong

Su wrote from Wusong, saying: "Come! Although you are panting in the heat wave of one hundred and one degrees, here, we are living in two seasons. Summer is a fully dressed young woman. Why are you losing the opportunity to be intimate with her? We have cicada songs, sunlight, and green sea water here. At night, there is even a half-moon. Come, come!"

Because of the charm of that bridge, I brought some light luggage and was taken to Wusong by a small steam train.

The scenery of the seaside is extremely poetic. Su and I walked on the small path of fine gravel. The lush grass brushed my clothes. Above was the eternally still blue sky. In the distance was the vast, endless sea with fine waves. At the junction of the sky and the sea, a few white sails were lazily moving forward in the breeze. A touch of purple in the sunset glow was extremely beautiful. In the reflected light, all the houses, roads, leaves, people, and livestock were covered with a strange and fascinating golden color. I felt like I was walking into a landscape painting with the confusing mood of a Dutch painter.

In the evening, everyone wandered on the coast, watching the sky darken so lovely (not terribly). The sea, the shore, and the people on the shore were all lost in the misty night fog. Along the snake-like long dike made of stone slabs, with a slightly hopeful mood, counting the quiet stone slabs, we walked past, like a hero in a myth, searching for the treasure guarded by demons in an unknown land. The seawater was churning day and night, gnawing at the rocks at the foot of the dike, playing wonderful music like cymbals and drums. Sitting quietly at the end of the long dike, listening to the endless waves surging under my feet, watching the stars shining, appearing, disappearing, and falling in the clear July sky, I seemed to be reciting a harmonious poem composed of the universe and all things. The sea breeze slowly blew from the direction of the weather station, carrying the singing of someone, I tilted my head and listened quietly, the more I listened, the more I felt intoxicated. The sad melody almost blended with the current scenery. When the singing stopped and I turned my head, we were surrounded by the hazy moonlight at some point.

On such a bright moonlit night, sitting in such a secluded corner of the sea where no one can reach, listening to the songs of even people, without saying a word, we suspected that we were having an ancient and magical dream!

In the dream, the great Shanghai, encompassing millions of people, was spewing venomous snake-like flames into the sky. That corner of the sky was entirely red. Under the red light, countless people were singing, crying, enjoying themselves, committing crimes, suffering, and harboring hope—an eternal struggle of life that continues uninterrupted...

What shattered our fantasies was an incomparably huge steamship, rushing out of the sea mouth like a behemoth, emitting smoke. The smoke and the night fog curled together. All that could be seen was the lights on the ship. With just one stop, we heard a heavy anchoring sound like a roar. The sound seemed to shake everything around. In an instant, it returned to silence. Our fantasies were resurrected again with the gentle call of the sea waves.

News 208

Since the organization of the Great Nature Singing Troupe in March, it has broadcast special programs on major radio stations and has been well received by all walks of life. Recently, many listeners have written letters requesting to join. In order to connect listeners' singing interests, the troupe welcomes those who have a good impression of the troupe to join. Please first send a letter to Miss Mary, Post Office Box 157. If suitable, you will be invited for an interview.

The Vienna Music Singing Society, organized by Mr. Zhang Yilu, will soon broadcast the latest famous movie songs. The society previously appointed Mr. Ma Bo as the leader, Mr. Xiao Peilin as the social director, and Mr. Ni Bao and Mr. Ni Maozhang as the officers. The female singers hired include Miss Zhang Yan, Lv Yin, Liao Yan, Ni Ying, etc. The orchestra specially hired the famous Mr. Zhu Xing to guide. It is understood that the society wants to recruit several female members. Those who are interested in singing are welcome to visit the society for an interview. The address of the society is No. 14 Da Da Lane, across from the Aivin羲 Road Patrol Room, telephone number 32045.

The International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in view of the lack of statistics on domestic radio owners, hereby reiterates the order that a radio registration application form must be completed and submitted for registration before the end of August. The Shanghai Radio Research Society at No. 390 Nanjing Road (at the mouth of Wufu Lane) has specially obtained many copies of the registration application form from the International Telecommunications Bureau for all sectors to request registration and guide all registration procedures, specifically to serve those who have radios, and does not charge any fees. It is also heard that the society's repair department has gathered many specialized personnel to be responsible for repairing damaged radios, with low fees and fast delivery. Business has been very busy recently.

Movie News

Jin Cheng Premieres "Grace of a Beauty" 209

The new production "Grace of a Beauty" by Tianyi Film Company is directed by Wen Yimin, starring Lu Lixia, Li Ying, Wei Pengfei, Shen Yarlun, Zhang Zhenduo, etc. This film is based on the novel "Grace of a Beauty" by the famous novelist Zhang Henshui. The plot takes a singing and dancing troupe as the background, with joys and sorrows mixed, laughter and tears intertwined. Its depiction of urban love is especially penetrating. Famous singers Bai Hong, Liming Jian, Yan Fei, Zhou Xuan, Xu Jian, etc. have also joined in the show, making it even more splendid. The film is scheduled to be premiered at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater, which is filled with the fragrance of coldness, on the 27th of this month.

Dancing Stars and Singers in "Peach Blossom Dream" 210

"Peach Blossom Dream," directed by Du Yu of Shanghai Company, is a large-scale singing and dancing film with profound meaning. It has recruited dancing stars from the sea, such as Huang Hun, Xu Canying, Cai Yiming, Fan Lixiang, Pan Wenjuan, Weng Lanhun, Feng Feng, Jia Qiuyun, etc., and singers such as Bao Xuexue, Lai Ling, Zhang Ru, Lin Ying, Manna, Lucy, Lv Yin, Xue Lian. The groups participating include the Plum Blossom Dance Troupe, Leng Yan Society, Silver Moon Dance Troupe, China Hibiscus Troupe, Rose Troupe, Nightingale Art Society, Mei Ling Troupe, Xinhua Opera Society. The talent is so great that it can be ranked first among domestic singing and dancing films.

Cathay Premieres "Symphony of Two Hearts" 211

The long-rumored "Symphony of Two Hearts" Two Hearts in Walt Time has been scheduled to be premiered at the Cathay Grand Theater on Avenue Joffre today (Saturday). The film stars Carl Brisson, who leaped from a singing star to a movie star. Although he has only starred in three films, "The Ring", "The Private Life of the Emperor", and this "Symphony of Two Hearts," his suave attitude has long been deeply imprinted in the minds of thousands of movie fans. "Symphony of Two Hearts" takes love as the warp and singing and dancing as the weft. The background is beautiful, the scenes are grand, and the description of how men pursue women and how women deal with men is particularly profound. When this film was produced, the film company specially invited Francesca, a red singer famous in Europe and America for her singing and dancing skills, to play the heroine in the film, so both the singing and the dancing are original and completely different from ordinary singing and dancing films. The picture below is a scene from the film.

Sun Shiyi's Dirge for Nie Er 212

The young composer Nie Er drowned in the sea off Kugenuma Beach in Fujisawa Town, Kanagawa Prefecture, Japan, on the night of the 17th of this month. His body is missing. His memorial service is currently being prepared and launched in Shanghai. His close friend Sun Shiyi, with unlimited sorrow, wrote a dirge, which has been set to music by Lü Ji. It will be printed and distributed soon. Here is the original version of Sun's dirge:

Dirge for Nie Er Sun Shiyi

The wind is calling,

The sea is roaring,

The waves are beckoning;

When the night is deep,

The moon is shining in the long sky,

Young friend—he,

Threw himself into the embrace of the ocean;

Swallowed in the raging waves and high tide

How could I have imagined?

From now on, farewell forever!

From now on, we have been deprived of our ambitious hero;

From now on, we are missing you at our outpost.

From now on, drifting where, far away from the homeland!

From now on, longing for people thousands of miles away, only dreams are distant!

Great ambitions are thrown away,

Heart and soul are not in vain.

Listen to thousands of people singing the heroic songs you composed,

You should be smiling in the underworld.

Facing the shocking bad news,

Looking at the boundless waves,

Do you know that your friends in your homeland, today,

With broken hearts, are mourning you!
